Task instruction sent to agent 
# Kafka Connect REST API v1 to v2 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Connect REST API: the v1 connector resource handlers, the v2 connector resource handlers, and the version routing logic. Identify what changed between v1 and v2 in the task status and error response schemas.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

55-usertext-
Search the /workspace/kafka--0753c489 directory for all Kafka Connect REST API implementations, specifically looking for:
1. v1 and v2 connector resource handlers/classes
2. Version routing logic that differentiates between v1 and v2 APIs
3. Task status response schemas that differ between versions
4. Error response schemas that differ between versions

Start by searching for patterns like:
- Files containing "v1" or "v2" in REST/API context
- Files in paths like */rest/resources/* or */rest/api/*
- Files related to task status, connector status, and error messages
- Any files that implement version routing or API versioning

Explore thoroughly and report all files found.

   202→
   203→        Slf4jRequestLogWriter slf4jRequestLogWriter = new Slf4jRequestLogWriter();
   204→        slf4jRequestLogWriter.setLoggerName(RestServer.class.getCanonicalName());
   205→        CustomRequestLog requestLog = new CustomRequestLog(slf4jRequestLogWriter, CustomRequestLog.EXTENDED_NCSA_FORMAT + " %{ms}T");
   206→        jettyServer.setRequestLog(requestLog);
   207→
   208→        /* Needed for graceful shutdown as per `setStopTimeout` documentation */
   209→        StatisticsHandler statsHandler = new StatisticsHandler();
   210→        statsHandler.setHandler(handlers);
   211→        jettyServer.setHandler(statsHandler);
   212→        jettyServer.setStopTimeout(GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN_TIMEOUT_MS);
   213→        jettyServer.setStopAtShutdown(true);
   214→
   215→        try {
   216→            jettyServer.start();
   217→        } catch (Exception e) {
   218→            throw new ConnectException("Unable to initialize REST server", e);
   219→        }
   220→
   221→        log.info("REST server listening at {}, advertising URL {}", jettyServer.getURI(), advertisedUrl());
   222→        URI adminUrl = adminUrl();
   223→        if (adminUrl != null)
   224→            log.info("REST admin endpoints at {}", adminUrl);

  - Path: `/connectors`
  - Methods: Handles CRUD operations, status, task management, restart, pause/resume operations
  - Key endpoints:
    - GET `/connectors` - List connectors
    - POST `/connectors` - Create connector
    - GET `/connectors/{connector}/status` - Get connector status
    - GET `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status` - Get task status

- **ConnectorPluginsResource.java** - Plugin validation and configuration
  - Path: `/connector-plugins`
  - Methods: Plugin validation and config retrieval

- **InternalConnectResource.java** - Internal inter-cluster communication
  - Path: `/connectors` (internal only)
  - Methods: Inter-worker communication for task configs and zombie fencing

- **InternalClusterResource.java** - Base class for internal cluster operations
  - Contains inter-worker communication handlers

- **LoggingResource.java** - Admin resource for logging configuration

173-assistanttext-
I have completed my analysis of the Kafka Connect REST API in the apache/kafka repository. Here's what I found:

## Key Finding

**The Kafka Connect REST API does NOT implement separate v1 and v2 API versions.** Instead, it uses a single unified REST API with backward-compatible changes.

## Summary of Findings

### REST Resource Handlers
I identified all main connector resource handlers:
- **ConnectorsResource** - Main connector management at `/connectors` path
- **RootResource** - Root endpoints and health checks
- **ConnectorPluginsResource** - Plugin validation
- **InternalConnectResource** - Inter-worker communication
- **ConnectRestServer** - Main server that registers all resources without version-specific paths

### Task Status Response Schema
Located in `ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState` with fields:
- `id` (int)
- `state` (string)
- `worker_id` (string)
- `msg` (string)
- `version` (string, optional - tracks plugin version, not API version)

### Error Response Schema
Located in `ErrorMessage` with fields:
- `error_code` (int)
- `message` (string)

### Version Field Usage
The `version` field in status responses (through `AbstractStatus` class) tracks **connector/task plugin versions**, not REST API versions. It's conditionally included in JSON responses.

### Version Routing
There is **no version routing logic** for API v1 vs v2. All requests go to the same endpoints, and versioning is managed through:
1. Backward-compatible schema changes
2. Plugin version tracking system
3. The Versioned interface for connectors

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file paths and relevant symbols.

Status Response Schemas\n\n**Task Status Classes:**\n- **TaskStatus.java** - Represents task runtime status\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/TaskStatus.java`\n  - Extends AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\n  - Fields: id, state, workerUrl, generation, trace, version\n\n- **ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState** - JSON response format for task state\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java`\n  - Fields: id, state, worker_id, msg, version\n\n**Connector Status Classes:**\n- **ConnectorStatus.java** - Represents connector runtime status\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/ConnectorStatus.java`\n  - Extends AbstractStatus<String>\n  - Fields: id (connector name), state, workerUrl, generation, trace, version\n\n- **ConnectorStateInfo.ConnectorState** - JSON response format for connector state\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java`\n  - Fields: state, worker_id, msg, version\n\n**Base Status Class:**\n- **AbstractStatus.java** - Base class for all status objects\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractStatus.java`\n  - Contains State enum: UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED\n  - Contains version field (nullable) for tracking plugin versions\n\n### 4. Error Response Schemas\n\n- **ErrorMessage.java** - Standard error response format\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java`\n  - Fields: error_code (int), message (String)\n\n- **ConnectRestException.java** - Exception class for REST errors\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectRestException.java`\n  - Tracks both HTTP status code and custom error code\n\n- **ConnectExceptionMapper.java** - Mapper for converting exceptions to REST responses\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java`\n  - Maps NotFoundException, AlreadyExistsException, and generic exceptions to appropriate responses\n\n- **BadRequestException.java** - Bad request exception\n  - Located at: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/BadRequestException.java`\n\n### 5. Instead:\n\n1. **Plugin Version Tracking**: The `version` field is tracked in status responses (TaskState, ConnectorState, AbstractStatus) for plugin versioning, not API versioning\n2. **Versioned Interface**: Located at `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java` - Used for plugin versioning\n3. **ConnectRestExtension Interface**: Located at `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java` - Allows extensions to be versioned\n4. **Test Plugins**: Version testing found in `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/test/resources/test-plugins/read-version-from-resource-v1/` and `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/test/resources/test-plugins/read-version-from-resource-v2/` - These test version reading capabilities but are NOT API version implementations\n\n### 7.
